I need to determine which candidates can be made equivalent to the Ground Truth:

**GT: c0*P*sin(c1*t) + c2*P*exp(-c3*t)**

This equals `P * [A*sin(B*t) + C*exp(-D*t)]` where A, B, C, D are fixed positive constants.

Key observations:
- GT is **linear in P** (every term has exactly P as a factor)
- GT has exactly two basis functions of t: `sin(B*t)` and `exp(-D*t)`
- No constant offset, no cos terms (unless phase-shifted), no log terms, no P² terms

**Candidate 11: P*c0*sin(c1*t + c2) + P*c3*exp(c4*t)**
= P*[c0*sin(c1*t + c2) + c3*exp(c4*t)]
Setting c2=0, c0=0.2569..., c1=0.7218..., c3=0.1149..., c4=-0.03038...
This matches GT exactly.
Candidate 11 verdict: [MATCH]

**Candidate 12: P*c0*cos(c1*t + c2) + P*c3*exp(c4*t)**
cos(c1*t + c2) = sin(c1*t + c2 + π/2). Setting c2 = -π/2 gives sin(c1*t). This matches GT.
Candidate 12 verdict: [MATCH]
